      uniform vec4 matColorDiffuse;       uniform vec4 matColorSpecular;      uniform vec4 matColorEmissive;      uniform float matShininess;         uniform float alphaTestRef;         uniform float scaleUV;                                                  varying vec3 refCoord;              varying vec2 texCoord2D;            varying vec3 v_normal;                                                  varying vec3 v_light0Vector;
